Bada ana aneya i toirubai, “Awaika kairavina am donkey nikosi mara tonu ku ravi? Yauku a botu am keta ata gudui kairavina am wagawaga kuriku kega gairena.
Ba donkey i kitaiku wai nikosi mara tonu i utusaira ba kega wai karaku ata kasibunuim ba donkey ita mana.”
Damanina ba Balaam Bada ana aneya i wonei, “Yauku piragagoyo a wosei, kega a kuiri kata ketai ku bimsiri kata kuti gesiku. Kega ke binuwagaire wai kata ana veramaga.”
Bada ana aneya Balaam i wonei, “Nikosi pipiya yabata ko nae saba, awaika ana wonim wai kona, wata ki sisiyei.” Damanina ba Balaam, Balak ana babadisi damana yabata si nae.























Balaam i peroveta wona: “Balak, ke bomsiri, ba ki tainabaenega, Zippor natuna ke nonoriku.
God wai kega pipiya mom kata ita kwaruma, kona pipiya mom natusi kata ana nota ita birai. Meyana i sisiya ba kega i wosei? Meyana i kaobiyoyobanim ba kega i wosei?
I kaotuneiku ani gairena, ba kona i gairenisi ba kega rubana ani neveramagei.
Kega goyona Jacob ana rakaraka kamonai kega goyona sina paiwarei Israel kamonai, kairavina Bada asi God kosi yabata, si yoneyonei kona asi taupauma kamosi yai.
Egypt yai God i yaunisi si kasibau, asi maragata garaga bull rutainina.
Kairapu kega rubana Jacob ina bowai, kega rubana sina pasiri Jacob ba Israel sini sisiyisi, ‘Ko kinani awaika God i wose!’
Nikosi dam lion bibituwana rutainina te kokona kega tema binubaisi yepo kasi sirage te bowabowai ba tarana te tomatomani.”






















“A kinani, saba kega karaku; A kitakitai saba kega gwabiku ai Jacob karinai gwamegwame ina kasibau ba Israel karisi yai ana nimakona putuputu ina kasibau Moab nao bakobakosi ina guda ba Seth natunatuna gayamisi ini kasigaoworana.
Edom sina yauni, ba kasi abiya Seir, sina getawani, saba Israel ini maragata.
Jacob karinai kaiwabo ina kasibau, ba pipiya si ma boterisi wai ina kasibigoyonisi.”






Israel biyisi Shittim meyaginai si mamana wai, sebasebare si dagui Moab bibaine yabata si raukaipara.
Si yorisi asi god kurina si puyopuyo bunuwa. Ba sibi kam poragana ba asi god si bopepetei.
Bada i yagisi saki kurisi kairavina Israel kurisi mena si kapu ba Peor asi god Baal si bopepetei.
Bada Moses kurina i wona, “Nikosi pipiya asi babada ereonowasi ke yaunisi ba ki kasibunuwana ba kao ai matakuai, ki debisi kata kega Bada ini yagisi saki Israel biyisi kurisi.”
Kata Moses Israel asi bibuibuiya biyisi si wonisi, “Komi iyabomi wata ami pipiya gaburimi yai, si kapu ba Peor asi god Baal te bopepetei wai, koi kasibunuwana.”
Moses ba Israel biyisi ereonowasi Tabernacle matam ketanai si tutou ba matasi yai Israel sebare midian wasike i urabai i botu ana rakaraka kurisi.
Maranai Eleazar natuna Phinehas Aaron wawana kona wai priest,
ba nikona i kinani wai koroto i kasibau taveyei ba yaronai ana iyo i yauni sebarena i kibi i riu ana ku gweda ba i yowa wai asi ruwamo i tupa kokonisi sebare ba wasike, kata Israel biyisi kasi gubaga i kakaba,
saba matapa pipiya asi 24,000 si rabobo.
Bada Moses kurina i wona,
“Eleazar natuna Phinehas kona wai priest ba Aaron wawana, au yagisi Israel biyisi gwabisi yai i tere sirei, kona yauku bokuwaiku kairavina i nuwarauwa kosi kamosi yai, kata au waina ata wosei wai kega a wosei.
Karaku ke wonei kata au nuwanuba bidamanina maragasina kurina ana wosei.
Niko bidamanina maragasina kamonai, kona ba ana rakaraka mara murinai te botubotu wai priest saibirina kamosi yai ina madamana, kairavina ana God kana waba bokuwayina kairavina i nuwarauwa ba Israel biyisi asi goyona i maisa taveyei.”
























































































Kata Bada Moses kurina i wona, “Nun natuna Joshua au kanuma i bonuwei wai ke yauni ba yarom ku gayamina ke terei.
Ke botuwei priest Eleazar ba pipiya ereonowasi naosi yai ini misiri ba kuni yonayona kata karaku, kona pipiya ini naovisi.
Am bibadana maragasina mutuna ki garubonei kurina kata Israel biyisi ereonowasi sina bosisirei.
Kona wai priest Eleazar naoni i nimsiri ba kona kairavina Urim ina toirubai awaika wata Bada naonai ina wose. Kata kona ina kaotuneisi wai Israel biyisi ereonowasi sina kasibau ba yebo sina riu.”
Moses mekabage Bada i kaotunei wai i wosei. Joshua i yauni ba priest Eleazar ba Israel biyisi ereonowasi naosi yai i msiri.
Damanina ba yarona gayamina tepanai i terei ba i yoneyonei Bada Moses i kaobiyoyobani wai nanakasike.








































































































































































































































Moab guburinai Jordan okowina parinai ba Jericho sepinai si kwanatu maranai, Bada Moses kurina i wona,
“Israel biyisi kurisi nikasike ki sisiya, ‘Maranai Jordan okowina koni gagubonei ku Canaan wai,
pipiya ereonowasi kona kupurinai te mamana wai ko kwabinisi sina kasibau. Asi tarabibisaka tebo pepeta ba asi bopepeta gawarisi koi kasi rikeyana.
Ba tano ko yauni ba namai ko kwanatu kairavina a berimi ini karimi yai.
Tanona aba binebinena ami dam nununai koi yapara owaowa. Koroto kaikapona wai yapara kaikapona ko berisi ba koroto yogiyogina wai yapara yogiyogina ko berisi. Ba kotoi aba binebinena sini garui ba ina binei wai karinai. Ami dam nununai koi yabei.
Pipiya namai te mamana wai kega kona kwabinsi ba kona boterisi sina mana wai matami sini siwa gaoworana ba ruriruri rutainina gabagabami sini siwa kwariyana. Ba kupurinai kona mana wai kosi sini abiyimi.
Ba kega kona kwabinisi sina kasibau wai mekabage a nosinosi ata kasibigoyonisi wai komi nakasike ana kasibigoyonimi.’”





































Ba Bada Moses kurina i wona,
“Maranai Jordan koni garubonei ku Canaan wa,
meyaga mutusi ke bineisi kata bosusura meyagisi, memena bage pipiya kega ana waina pipiya ita kasibunui saba i kasibunui wai ina vera kona ku mayagina ina bosusura.
Kosi meyagisi wai aba kobakoba gawarisi, biuwa yaunina kairavina pipiyina kega ina bosusura. Kata kasibunuwa biyina kega ina rabobo ba koroto ai, sina kai bibuibuiyei.”



















































































































































Damanina ba Moses Israel biyisi kurisi i wona, “Kairuwana ereonowana ani beyebeyimi wai ko bosisirana wai kona mana ba kona riu ami kupura Bada ami God e bereberimi wai kona yauni ba ini karimi yai.
Kega nikosi kaotunetune tepanai sisiya kona tubotaini kona kesana kona botaveyei. Saba Bada ami God ana kaotunetune a bereberimi wai ko bokikisi.



Ko bosisirana kabitamnisi kata dam mutusi parimi ai ami nuwasuya ba kuira sina kitai. Ba nikosi kaotunetune sina nonora ba sina wona, ‘Bisuwona, niko dam kaikapona, wai pipiyisi nuwanuwasuyisi ba kuikuirisi!’
Kega dam kesana kaikapona asi god e gwabigwabisi nanakasike bage kota ata Bada God maranai ta raupari kurina wai gwabiti ai e mamana.
Nikosi kairuwana karaku a wonewonim wai totorisi ba gaire sakiyisi. Kega meo dam kesana kaikapona ana kairuwana totorisi ba gaire sakiyisi bage niko kairuwana karaku a bereberimi wai rutainina.























Maranai Bada ami God Egypt yai ana maragata kaikaponai i uraba kasibauwimi, kiyakiyaya ba wose kaikaposi i wose. Ba komi kairavimi Egypt i abiyisi ba paiwara kaikapona i berisi. I wosimi ikesina mom ana pipiya, ba Sainai koyanai keyama kai karakarasina basunai ko nonori i sisiya kurimi ba katai yawayawasimi ko mamana. Nikasike wose kainaona i tupuwa kona kega? Kega! Ko nuwasuya e veramaga God pipiya dobuai i wosisi maranai, dobu ereonowana ko kinani. Kega god kesana nikasike wose i wose.
<range>
<range>




Kata Bada kona sapama kaidamonai ba dobu gaburinai kana God, ba kega memena kesana kotoi. Kona kairavina karaku ke nosi ba nuwanuwami yai e mana.
Ba nikosi kairuwana ba kaotunetune karaku a bereberimi wai ko bokikisi kata komi ba natunatumi sina tupuwa wai gairenai wata ba Bada ami God kupura e bereberimi wai kona mamanei yepo ami mara ku damona.”













































“Ko nonora, Israel biyimi! Bada ata God kona Bada kesana.
Bada ami God koi nuwayauyauni, nuwanuwami tupanai, pipiyimi tupanai ba ami maragata tupanai.
Nikosi kairuwana karaku a bereberimi wai nuwanuwami yai sina mana.
Natunatumi koi beyena tupetupenisi. Yove yai kona mamana wai koi sisiyei, ba ketai kona yewoyewo wai, ba kona kenokira ba kona bomsiri maranai wai koi sisiyei.”


















“Maranai Bada ami God ina urabaimi kona riu ba niko kupura kona yauni wai dam pesarisi naomi yai ina kwabisi sina kasibau. Kosi Hitti biyisi, Girgashi, Amori, Canaan, Perizi, Hivi ba Jebusi biyisi, dam asi 7 si rakata saki ba si maragata saki kega bage komi.
Ba maranai Bada ami God ku yaromi ina terisi ba kona gebinubaisi wai koni subikakabisi, kega kesana kona boterei. Kega koni turaturanisi ba kega koni nuwanuwanisi.
Kega kosi pipiyisi yabata kona tabine. Kega natunatumi bibaine kona kaotaveyisi natunatusi sebasebare yabata sina tabine, kona natunatumi sebasebare kona kaotaveyisi natunatusi bibaine yabata sina tabine,
muri yai ba natunatumi sebasebare sini nuwatainisi ba god mutusi sina bopepetisi wai, Bada yana ina borabora saki wai yagiyaginai wata ina kasibigoyonimi.
Nikasike kurisi kona wosei. Asi raunabonabo koi kasi rikeyana ba, asi akima bobokuwayisi koi kasigaoworana, ba Asherah ana ariri koi tara kotobana ba asi tarabibisaka keyama karakarasinai ko kapuna.
Kairavina Bada ami God kurina wai komi pipiya kaobaisiyemi. Dobu tompipininai pipiya ereonowasi kamosi yai, Bada ami God i bineimi kata komi ana pipiya ba ana sawara monimonikina.
Bada i wainimi ba i bineimi ba kega ko pesara kairavina, komi wai ami koroto i yogiyogi saki kega bage dam mutusi
Bada i nuwayauyaunimi ba ana kaobiyoyobana maragasina kairavina i wosei.
Kona kuiri kata Bada ami God, kona God. Kona God bipatutu biyina awaika i wonei wai e wosewosei ba nuwayauyauna bidamanina maragasina e botawani kimta thousand kurisi iyabosi te binuwayauyauni ba ana kaotunetune te botawani.
Saba iyabosi te bisinikikiyei wai yagiyagina wata saroba ina berisi ba ina kasibigoyonisi.
Kona kairavina ko kinani kata nikosi kaotunetune, biyoyobana ba kairuwana, karaku a berebereim wai ko kibi kabitam.”















“Ko pota kabitamni kata nikosi kaotunetune ereonowasi karaku a bereberimi wai kona kibi kata kona mana, ba koni tuwa pesara, ba kona riu ba Bada nosinosimi kurisi i kaobiyoyobana wai kupurina kona yauni ba ini karimi yai.
Ko nosi, mekabage Bada ami God bodu 40 i naovimi kupura momna kamonai kata ita terimi koi moyaka meyimi ba i rurubaimi kata ita kuiri awaika nuwanuwami yai ba yebo ana kaotunetune kota bosisirana kona kega.
I wosimi koi moyaka ba soya ko rabobo saba manna i kanikanimi, saba niko kam wai, komi ba wawami yabata kega ko kuiri. Nikona i wosei wai i bibeyimi kata pipiya kega kam wata sina kani ba sina mana, saba wona ereonowana Bada kawanai e kasikasibau wai, konai tana mana.








Ba saba maranai ko kamkam siyabagi wai, yove yawayawana ko bowabowa ba ko mabinubaimi,
ba ami cow ba sheep asi koroto te rakarakata ba, ami silver ba gold te pesapesara ba ami sawara ereonowasi te pesapesara saki,
ko kinani kata kega kona netagegeyim, ba Bada ami God kuni notawapei, Egypt kupurinai patuma kamonai i urabakasibauwimi.
Kairavinai naovimi nao kupura momna kaikapona ba aba naganagarina, okowina kega, ba memei mota bikokonisi ba rido yabata, ba akima padapadana kamonai okowa kairavimi i wosei i kasibau.
Ba kupura mominai manna tutunumi si buruburuwei wai i kanimi ba i wosimi koi moyaka kata i rurubaimi mara murinai komi ami gairena kairavina.
Abisiri yai kuna wona, ‘Yauku ikesiku au maragatai ba au sini nubanubai ba yaroku ai niko mariya a panani.’
Saba Bada ami God ko nosi, kairavina kona maragata i berimi wai ko mariya, ba ana bidamanina maragasina nosinosimi yabata kurisi i wosei wai i bokikisi yepo i botu karaku.
Abisiri yai Bada ami God koni nota gugei ba god mutusi koni saunurisi, ba kona bopepetisi ba kona rudune kurisi wai karaukarau ana kaorumatanimi ba ana kasibigoyonimi.
Kata dam mutusi naomi yai Bada i kasibigoyonisi wai, komi Bada ami God kega kona bosisirei wai nanakasike ina kasibigoyonimi.”




































































“Nikosi au wona nuwanuwami yai ba ami nota ai tema kabitam, ba matakira gubana kairavina wai nimami yai ko kauta ba nao bakobakomi ai ko kote.
Natunatumi koi beyebeyisi, maranai yove yai kona mamana kona ketai kona yewoyewo, ba kona kenokira ba kona bomsiri wai, koi sisiyei.






Karaku nina naomi yai bigairena ba kaonawa a tereterei.
Maranai Bada ami God ana kaotunetune karaku a bereberimi kona bosisiri wai ini gairenimi.
Ba maranai Bada ami God ana kaotunetune karaku a bereberimi ketana koni sumarei ba god mutusi kega ko kuira ba ko kibikibisi wai ina kaonawaimi.



Ko kinana kabitamni kata nikosi bai yoyobana ba kairuwana karaku a berebererimi wai ereonowasi ko bosisirana.”









































































































































“Maranai kona riu kupura Bada ami God e bereberimi wai kona yauni ini karimi yai, ba kona mabinubaimi, ba kona wona, ‘Ko kinani kata taupauma kesana tana terei ina potaita nikosi dam si mabisubibirita wai rutainisi.’
Ko kita kabitamni kata taupauma kona binei wai Bada ami God ana binebinena, komi waresimi kesana kamomi yai kona binei. Ba kega pipiya tumana kotoi kega Israel biyina kona binei ina potaimi.
Ba taupauma wai kega ikesina kairavina horse pesarisi ina yauna, ba kega pipiya ina wosisi sina veramaga ku Egypt yebo mutusi sina gimona, kairavina Bada i wona, ‘Komi kega nao ku kupura kona veramaga mena.’
Kona kega kaokaowana pesarisi ina yauna muri yai ba nuwanuwana BADA karinai sina taina sirei, kona kega mariya ini sasaranei, ba silver ba gold ina yauna saki.
Maranai taupauma asi aba makimakirai ina makira wai, ikesina kairavina niko kaotunetune tupana Livai biyisi kairuwana pepana sina berei wai ina kirumi.
Ba gwabinai ina botawani ba kao patepatena ana yawasa kamonai ina baibaiyavi kata Bada ana God ina kuira kabitamni ba ina bokuwayei ba ana kairuwana sisiyisi ina kibi kabitamni.
Ba kega ina nota meyei kata kona wai i gaire saki kega turaturana mutusi rutainisi ba Bada ana kairuwana ini kawapatei ba ana wainai wata ina nae. Kata kona ba ana rakara murinai te botubotu wai Israel kamonai asi bi taupauma marana ina veoroma.”








“Maranai kona riu kupura ami God e bereberimi wai, kega dam namai te mamana wai asi yawasa pudapudasi ba goyo tavetaveyisi koni boneboneisi.
Kega kesana kamomi yai sina panani natuna sebare kona wasike raunabonabo tepanai keyama karakarasinai ina puyobunuwa, ini kairapu, ina yapune, ini kwerikweri, kona ini muwara,
kona te kawakawa kairapu ba raoboraobosi kanumisi te yoreyoeyore geyisi ba yoveyovesi ba banebanesi.
Kotoi wata nikosi wose pudapudasi ina wose wai Bada kurina wai; si goyo saki. Ba nikosi wose goyogoyosi kairavina Bada ami God naomi yai dam ina kwabinisi sina kasibau.
Komi Bada ami God matanai kega awaika kunumakina kona yauni.”

“Ba komi kairavimi wai Bada ami God peroveta yauku rutainiku. Warewaresimi kesana kamomi yai ina yorei ba kona, ana sisiya kona nonori.
Ba Sainai koyanai koi kesanimi wai Bada ami God koi babai maranai ko wona kata, ‘Kega Bada ata God gamona tana nonori kona niko keyama karakarasina tana kinana meyei, muri yai ba tana rabobo.’
Ba Bada kuriku i wona, ‘Awaika si sisiyei wai i gaire.
Yauku peroveta kesana Israel biyisi waresisi kamosi yai kom rutainim ana yorei, ba kawanai wonaku a kaotunei wai ereonowana pipiya ina wonisi.
Ba kotoi wata wonaku niko peroveta kau wabai ini biyoneyonei ba kega ina nonora wai yauku ikesiku mom saroba ana berei.
Saba meo peroveta kega sisiya a wonei ba kau wabai e bisisiya, kona god mutusi kasi wabai e bisisiya wai ko kasibunui.’
Saba memena bage kona wona, ‘Mekabage kana kuiri kata wara kega Bada i porai?’
Maranai peroveta Bada kana wabai e biyonayona ba wosena kega ina tupuwa wai, kona kuiri kata kona warana wai kega Bada i sisiya. Nao peroveta wai ikesina ana sisiya ba kega kona nagarei.”








































































































































































































































































































































Damanina ba Moses, Israel biyisi matasi yai Joshua i yorei ba i wonei, “Ki maragata ba ki tepatora. Kairavina kom nikosi pipiya yabata kona nae Bada nosinosisi kupura i kaobiyoyobana ita berisi wai nakai kona riu. Kom mom kupurina kamonai kuni yapara owaowa ba tanona kamosi yai kom kuni kodei kata asi buderi.
Ba Bada ikesina ini naovim ba ina potaim kega ini sumarimi kona ina tere bigaruimi ba kega kuna nagara, kona am nota ina peku.”







































































































Damanina ba Moses Moab guburinai wata i gae ku, Nebo koyana i gaeni ku Pisgah tepana Jericho sepinai. Ba Bada kupurina tupana Gilead yai ba i nae ku Dan wai ereonowana i beyei,
yebo i nae ku Naphtali ba Ephraim ba Manasseh kupurisi. Ba Judah kupurinai ba i kabari i nae ku Mediterranean Enagina.
Ba ku Negev kupura momna ba Jericho ku kawa sanagina ba ku Palm meyagina ba i nae Zoar parasina.
Damanina ba Bada, kurina i wona, “Niko kupura ikesiku mom au kaobiyoyobana maragasina a wosei, Abraham, Isaac ba Jacob kurisi, ba a wona, ‘Am rakaraka ana bereisi.’ Ai beyim matami yai ku kitai saba kom kega kuni garubona nakai.”
Kata Bada ana saibisaibirina Moses namai Moab kamonai i rabobo, Bada i wona wai nanakasike.



Kata Nun natuna sebare Joshua, nuwasuya kanumina i bonuwei kairavina Moses yarona gayamina tepanai i terei. Ba Israel biyisi si tainabaenega kurina, mekabage Bada, Moses i kaotunei wai nanakasike si wosei.



Ba Bada ana saibisaibirina Moses i rabobo murinai Bada Moses kana bibaita Joshua Nun natuna sebare kurina i wona,
“Au saibisaibirina Moses i rabobo. Karaku kom ba nikosi pipiya ereonowasi ko bobunaga ba Jordan okowina koni garubonei ba kupura Israel biyisi ana berisi wai nakai kona nae.
Yauku gawara ereonowana memena kaem kuna tereterei wai ana berim, Moses a kaobiyoyobani wai nanakasike.
Am kupura wai kupura momnai ina dagui ba ina nae ku Lebanon ba namai okowa kaikapona Euphrates ai ba i nae Hitti biyisi asi kupura Mediterranean Enagina ku mara sipuna mena.
Kega kesana kotoi am yawasa ereonowana kamonai ina gebeyim. Yauku Moses yabata wai yebo kesanina kom ba Yauku yabata, ba Yauku kega ani sumarim kona ana tere bigaruim.
Ki maragata ba ki tepatora kairavina nikosi pipiya kuni naovisi kata nosinosim a kaobiyoyobanisi kupura ata berisi wai ini karimi yai.
Ki maragata ba ki tepatora saki. Kairuwana ereonowana au saibisaibirina Moses a berei wai ko kinana kabitamni kata kona bosisirana; ba kega kesana kona vera taveyei wai birana gairena wata.
Niko kairuwana bukana kega kawami ina kasibau taveyei; kao ba pom kona nota bitetei wai kamonai ereonowana si kirumi wai kona wose roboi wai kona mariya ba awaika kona wosei wai ereonowana gairena wata.”



















































































Damanina ba Bada Joshua kurina i wona, “Karaku Egypt patuma sinimayina a kasikasipupuni.” Kona kairavina niko kupura kana waba Gilgal ba karaku patana te yoreyorei Gilgal.
Kata Israel biyisi Gilgal siru basekwa Jericho guburinai, ba rabisi yai kao kana bi 14 ba nawaravi dagudagunai Baisaubona Kamna si wosewosei.
Mara itom Baisaubona Kamna murinai kupurinai grain si boyauna ba si kapukapuna ba bread kega yeast yabata si kani.
Niko kam si kanikani ba mara i tomtom wai manna i kakaba ba Canaan kupurinai awaika si bobaoni wai kona si kani.


















































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































Damanina ba Joshua Israel biyisi asi dam nununai Shechem meyaginai i runotuwanisi. Ba wara i porapora asi magumagura, babada, bibuibuya biyisi ba abiya babadisi sita botu God naonai si gaenisi.
Ba Joshua pipiya ereonowasi kurisi i wona, “Bada Israel biyisi asi God nikasike i wona, ‘Matapa naki tamatamami naki, Abraham ba Nahor tamasi Terah yabata Euphrates okowina sepinai si mamana ba god mutusi si bopepetisi.
Ba yauku tamami Abraham kupura okowa sepinai a yauni ba Canaan kupurinai wata ai naovei ba natuna Isaac kamonai ana rakaraka pesarisi a berei.









Kata kupura a berimi wai tano kega ko baoni ba meyaga kega ko bowai, saba kamosi yai ko mamana ba vine ba olive keyamisi kega ko bao ba kamsi ko kamkam.’
Karaku Bada ko kumarei ba nuwanuwami tupanai ko bosaibiri. God mutusi nosinosimi Euphrates okowina sepinai, ba Egypt kamonai si bopepetisi wai koi garugaru, ba Bada ko bosaibiri.
Saba Bada bosaibirina sinimi ina kai wai, karaku niko kaonai kairavimi ko binei kata kotoi kona bosaibiri, abisiri yai god mutusi okowa sepinai nosinosimi si bosaibirisi wai, kona Amori biyisi asi god, asi kupurai ko mamana wai kosi. Saba yauku ba au rakaraka wai Bada kana bosaibisaibiri.”
Damanina ba pipiya si kaobeya, “Yakai kega rubarubana Bada kana boterei ba god mutusi kana bosaibisaibirisi!
Yakai Bada ama God ikesina Egypt kamonai tamatamakai yabata patuma kupurinai i uraba kasibauwikai, ba kiyakiyaya kaikaposi mataki ai i wose. Kona dam ba dam kamosi yai ama wagawaga ereonowanai i pota kabitamnikai.
Ba Bada naoki ai dam pesarisi i kwabinisi si kasibau, nanakasike Amori biyisi kupurinai si mamana wai, ba yakai yebo Bada kana bosaibiri basuna kona wai ama God.”

























































Joshua ana yawasa ereonowana kamonai Israel biyisi Bada, si bosaibisaibirei ba i rabobo murinai, pipiya warawaraetesi iyabosi wata si mamana wai, Bada Israel biyisi kairavisi wose kaikaposi i wosewose wai ereonowana si kinani.
Nun natuna Joshua, Bada ana saibisaibirina, kana bodu 110 ba i rabobo.
Ba ana buderi tanonai, Timnath Heres kana yapara si berei wai namai si dogui, Ephraim kupurinai, Gaash koyana ku yabarata mena.
Kona kimtina si rabobo murinai ba murina kimtina si rakata si gae wai Bada si buruburuwei ba sawara Israel biyisi kairavisi i wose wai kega si kuiri.
Kona kairavina Bada matanai goyona si wosewosei ba tarabibisaka Baal si bopepetisi.
Ba Bada, tutunusi asi God, kona Egypt kamonai i urabakasibauwisi wai si nota wapei. Kosi pipiya gwabisi yai asi god mutusi si kibikibisi ba, si bopepetisi. Kata kosi Bada si yagisigisiyei.
Ba Bada bopepetina si boterei ba Baal ba Ashtoreth si bopepetisi.
Ana yagisi kamonai i kaotaveyisi wai, kasi abiya si botu si ravisi ba asi sawara si sekwa roboisi kata, kega rubana sita gebeyisi.
Mara patepatena abiya kairavina si nenae wai, Bada kega i bibaisisi kata kasi abiya sita bobeyisi, mekabage i kaobiyoyobana wai nanakasike. Kata kosi si bokwarakwara saki.
Damanina ba Bada, bibuibuiya babadisi i berisi wai, Israel biyisi kasi abiya yarosi ai si yawasisi
Saba Israel biyisi kega si bosisirisi. Bada ku murisi si terei, ba kamosi yai sibi kakaiwaka ba god mutusi si bopepetisi.
Maranai Bada Israel biyisi bibuibuiya badana i bereberisi wai, Bada kona bibuibuiya badana yawayawasina i mamana wai, i bibaisi kata kasi abiya yarosi ai i biyawasisi, kairavina iyabosi si bobisipuvisi ba, si bobirasarasaisi wai Bada i kamyosukuvisi.
Ba maranai bibuibuiya badana i raborabo wai pipiya yebo si neveramaga asi ku yawasa wadubosi ba, god mutusi si bisaununurisi ba, si bosaibirisi ba si bopepetisi. Kega bage rorowa tutunusi rutainisi ba, nuwanuwasi si padapada kata, kega asi waina yawasa wadubosi sita botaura.








































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































Sebare kesana kana waba Elkana, kona wai Jeroam natuna ba Jeroam wai Elihu natuna ba Elihu wai Tohu natuna ba Tohu wai Zuph, Ephraim biyina natuna. Rama kupurinai i mamana Ephraim koyanai.
Elkana kaokaowana asi ruwamo. Hana ba Penina. Penina ere natunatuna ba Hana wai kaipokina.
Bodu patepatena Elkana i bowagawaga ku Shilo, bopepeta ba puyobunuwa kairavina, Bada Maragata Sakina kurina. Kona maranai Bada ana priest wai Ilai natunatuna ruwamo Hopni ba Phinehas.
Elkana ana puyobunuwa kaona maranai kaowana Penina ba natunatuna kasi ruburuma kesakesasike i bereberisi.
Saba Hana i nuwayauyauna sakiyei, kona kairavina kana koda wai kaikapona i bereberei, bagunai wata Bada God i kaipokiyei.
Ba Penina wai Hana ibiabiyei ba i kaobibisakei ba i binamei kairavina Bada i kaipokiyei.
Nikona, bodu patepatena i tuputupuwa, maranai si nenae Bada God ana ku yove. Ba Hana wai, i binuwapoya saki ba kega i kamkam.
Elkana kaowana kurina i wona, “Hana, awaika kairavina ke tutou, ba awaika kairavina kega ke kamkam, ba awaika kairavina nuwanuwam e goyogoyo? Yauku kurim wai nanakasike bage natunatum sebasebare asi 10 kom karimi yai.”
Mara kesana puyobunuwa kamna Shilo kamonai si kakabi wai, Hana i bomsiri. Priest Ilai wai aba makimakirai Bada ana yove matamketa gwabinai i makira i mamana.
Hana nuwanuwana yapoya i bobunui ba ere tou gabugabunuvina i bomsiri Bada kurina i rupari.
Hana i kaobiyoyobana i wona, “O Bada Maragata Sakina, yauku am aba saibisaibira, ke kinaniku! Au nuwayara ke kinani! Kega kuni notawapiku ba ke nosiku! Natuku sebare kuna beriku wai, ana yawasa tupana ana berim ina bosaibirim ba uyavina kega meyana sina tomni.”
Nanakasike i raupari ba Ilai wai kawana i bokibukibui.
Nuwa sinenai i bisisiya wai kega gamona i nonori, ba kipuruna wata i bokwayokwayo. Kona kairavina i nosi bage ita toma neganega.
I kaomainimainiyei i wona, “Awaika kairavina ke boneganega? Am toma neganega ke boterei.”
Hana i kaobeyei, “Bada, kega a toma neganega. Yauku wai nuwayara kaikapo sakina kamonai ba Bada God kurina nuwanuwaku a biutusewai.
Kega am saibisaibirina kuna nosi kata wasike neganegana; Au nuwapoya ba nuwagoyo kaikapona kamonai wai nina a raupari.”
Ilai i kaobeyei, “Nuwanubai ke nae, ba Israel biyisi asi God awaika kui babai wai ina berim.”
Ba kona i wona, “A bikaikaivim, bada, ba ke nota kabitamniku.” Damanina i nae ba i kam ba kega i nuwagoyo mena.
Mara i tom mena didibarinai ereonowasi si bomsiri si nae Bada God naonai si bopepeta ba si veramaga asi ku meyaga Rama. Elkana kaowana Hana yabata si dauwa, ba Bada God ana bibaba i nosi.
Ba kona murinai Hana i manawa ba sebare i tuwei. Ba kana waba i yorei Samuel, basuna i wona, Kona kairavina Bada God ai babai.
Ba yebo marana i botu wai, Elkana ana rakaraka yabata si gae mena sita puyobunuwa Bada kurina i kaobiyoyobana wai sita wosei.
Hana kega i nae, ba kaowana kurina i wona, “Niko sebareikei ani karamarei murinai ana yauni Bada ana berei ba namai mamanina ina mana.”
“Damanina, Elkana i kaobeyei awaika kurim i gaire wai ke wosei. Nimai kuna mamana ba kuni bitomani yepo kuni karamarei, ba Bada God ini baisim am kaobiyoyobana kuna wosei.”
Samuel i karamarei murinai, sinana i yauni i nae ku Shilo, bull wotuna kana bodu tonu ba flour 10 kg ba wine dubina kesana yabata.
Bull wotuna si puyobunuwa murinai sebareikei si yauni si nae Ilai kurina,
ba sinana i wona, “Bada, yauku mom rorowa a botu Bada kurina a raupari wai ku kinaniku.
Niko pipiyaikei kairavina a rupari ba Bada ai babai wai au bibaba i wosei.
Ba karaku nina Bada kurina a bereberena. Ana yawasa tupana a berebere taveyei.” Damanina ba namai Bada i bopepetei.
Damanina Hana i rupari Bada kurina ba i wona: “A binuwagaire Bada kurina au maragata i beriku. Kau abiya a pasapasa tawanisi, kairavina a binuwagaire saki kui yawasiku kairavina.
Kega kesana kotoi kaobaisiyena kom rutainim, Bada kega kesana kotoi rutainim e mamana, kega bopapara kesana kom rutainim, ama God.
Kau abiya kurina ana wona, ‘Kega kuna netagegeyim ba kuni sisiya gasegase ba am kaopasapasa ke boterei. Kairavina Bada kona God ba awaika ereonowana i kuiri ba wose e rubarubai.’
Iyo biyisi asi pidu i kotoba ba iyabosi mesumesusi i bobimaragasisi.
Kam siyabagisi karaku kam kairavina sina bagibagi, soya te raoboraobo wai karaku sina kam siyabagi. Wasike kaipokina pipiya asi 7 ini tuwisi ba sina, i tuwa pesara wai ina ma binuwana.
Bada rabobo e botubotuwei ba yebo e biyawasa; ku dogu e titaina kirei ba e bobimsiri.
Bada gomara ba mariya e biporai; ina tere kireim ba ina bokabarim.
Moyamoyakisi tano ai i bokabarisi ba isara bowabowasi si bikamyosukusuku wai babda yabata i makirisi, ba gawara kaobaisiyena wai, kosi karisi yai. Dobu kaena kona Bada God karinai, ba tepanai dobu i bowai.
Ana pipiya yapaikisi kaesi e bopapara, ba pipiya goyosi baidibarai sina boguguba. Kega ata maragatai ta mamana
Iyabosi Bada te gebeyei wai ini utu gaowogaoworisi. Sapamai waipararai ina gebeyisi; Bada dobu tupana ini buibuiyei. Ana taupauma maragata ina berei. Ba taupauma i boroi wai ina bobimaragasi.”
Elkana i veramaga ku Rama, ba sebareikei Samuel i mana ba Bada i bosaibisaibiri priest Ilai gaburinai.

























Samuel Bada kairavina Ilai gaburinai i saibisaibira. Ba kosi marasi yai Bada kega mamanina pipiya kurisi ibi sisiya kona meumeu ai i rerematara.
Pom kesana Ilai matana i goyogoyo kega rubarubana iti kinana kabitam wai ana gawarai i kenokira i dudauwa.
God ana yasegana kega i rabobo ba Samuel Bada ana yove kamonai Bada ana Bidamanina Maragasina Dedewagina parinai i kenokira.
Damanina ba Bada Samuel i yorei ba Samuel i kaobeyei, “Yauku nina.”
Ba i vera i nae Ilai kurina ba i wona, “Yauku nina.” Saba Ilai i wona, “Kega a yorim, ke veramaga kuna kenokira kuna dauwa.” Samuel i veramaga ba i kenokira.
Bada yebo i yore mena, “Samuel!” Ba Samuel i bomsiri i nae Ilai kurina ba i wona, “Ku yoriku wai yauku nina.” Ilai i wona, “Natuku, kega a yorim, ke veramaga kuna kenokira.”
Samuel Bada kega i kuiri kairavina kega meyana Bada i sisiya kurina.
Bada Samuel mara bitonuina i yorei, ba i bomsiri i nae Ilai kurina ba i wona, “Ku yoriku wai yauku nina.” Damanina ba Ilai i kuira taveyei kata Bada sebareikei i yoreyorei.
Kona kairavina Samuel i wonei, “Ke nae, ba kuna kenokira, ba ini yoereyana mena kurim wai ke wona, ‘Ki sisiya Bada, am saibisaibirina e bitainabaenega.’” Damanina Samuel i veramaga ba ana gawarai i kenokira.
Bada i botu i msiri ba i yoreyorei wai nanakasike i yoereyana “Samuel! Samuel!” Damanina ba Samuel i wona, “Ki sisiya am saibisaibirina e bitainabaenega.”
Ba Bada Samuel kurina i wona, “Sawara padapadana kesana Israel kamonai ana wosei ba pipiya sina nonori wai sina sikwana neganega.
Kona maranai Ilai ana rakaraka yabata ana kasibigoyonisi awaika ereonowana matapa a wonisi wai ana wosei.
A wonei kata ana rakaraka ani buibuiyena damanisi kairavina natunatuna asi piragagoyo i kuiri ba si bigigimiku saba, kega i gesisi.
Kona kairavina au kaobiyoyobana Ilai ana rakaraka yabata sina puyobunuwa kona sina suwara saba asi goyona kega meyana ana notataveyei.”
Samuel i kenokira i dudauwa yepo mara i tom ba Bada ana yove matam ketana i botaveyei. Awaika Bada i wonei wai, Ilai wonina i nagarei,
saba Ilai i yorei ba i wona, “Samuel, natuku.” Samuel i kaobeyei, “Yauku nina.”
Ilai i toiruba, “Awaika God i wonim? Tupana ke woniku. Kuni buniyei wai, Bada saroba kaikapona ina berim.”
Damanina Samuel kega kesana awaika i buniyei tupana i wone roboi. Damanina Ilai i wona, “Kona wai Bada God, ba awaika gairena matanai wai ina wosei.”
Bada wai Samuel gwabinai ba i rakata i gae ba awaika tupana i wonei wai i tupuwa.
Ba Israel ereonowasi Dan ba i nae ku Beersheba si kita taveyei kata Samuel wai Bada ana peroveta.
Bada mamanina Shilo ai i rerematara, ba namai wonanai i bimamatara meyei Samuel kurina.








































































Samuel i magura maranai, natunatuna sebasebare i bineisi Israel siti badei.
Iyarokona kana waba Joel ba murimurina kana waba Abijah, ba Beersheba kamonai si saibira.
Saba natunatuna kega ana wose si yauni; kosi wai mane si kirokirorowei. Ku kwaruma si riu wai keta totorina si siwani.
Kona kairavina Israel babadisi ereonowasi si notuwa ba si botu ku Rama Samuel kurina.
Si wonei, “Kom karaku kui magura saki ba natunatum kega am keta te kibikibi; wai ama taupauma ke binei ini naovikai dam mutusi rutainisi.”
Saba maranai si wona, “Taupauma ke berikai kata ini naovikai,” wai Samuel kega i nuwagaire; damanina Bada kurina i rupari.
Ba Bada i wonei, “Pipiya awaika ereonowana te wonewonim wai ke nonori; kega kom te bisinikikiyim saba yauku asi taupauma si sinikikiyiku.
Egypt yai au rabakasibauvisi maranai ba i botu karaku nina si kaosairiku ba god mutusi si bosaibirisi, wai kona wosena te wosewosei kurim.
Karaku ki tainabaenega kurisi; ba ke kaobiyoyobanisi ba ke wonisi sina kuiri kata mekabage taupauma ini badisi ba kega ina pota kabitamnisi.”
Samuel Bada ana sisiya ereonowana pipiya taupauma kairavina si baba wai i wonisi.
I wona, “Nikasike taupauma ini badimi ba ina wosei kurimi: Natunatumi sebasebare ina yaunisi ba chariot ba horse yabata sina bagibagi ba chariot naosi yai sina veravera.
Mutusi ini taunisi pipiya 1,000 sini badisi ba mutusi pipiya 50 sini badisi, ba mutusi ana tano sina robei ba sina bokuya ba yebo mutusi kapiya abiya kairavina ba chariot kasi sawara sina wose.
Ba natunatumi bibaine wai ina yaunisi ina ba kaomainimainisi bane wosewosesi ba bitaba ba kam sina gibu kairavina.
Ami kwapu marimariyisi, ba ami wine masawina ba olive masawina gaire sakina ana saibisaibira babadisi ina berisi.
Ami grain ba ami grape 10 kesana ina yauna taveyei ana aba potapota ba ana aba saibisaibirisi ina berisi.
Ami saibisaibirisi sebaresi ba bibainesi ba ami aba payapaya cow ba donkey kaimatanisi, kona kairavina sina saibira.
Ami aba payapaya sheep ba goat 10 kesana ina yauna ba komi yebo kairavina kona saibira.
Kona marana ina botu wai taupauma ko binei wai kurina kona tou rasarasa baiyawasimi kairavina, ba Bada kona maranai kega ini baisimi.”
Saba pipiya Samuel si kaosairei ba si wona, “Kega! Ama waina taupauma.
Kata dobu mutusi rutainisi taupauma ini naovikai ba yabata kana nae kama abiya naosi yai kani abiya.”
Maranai Samuel pipiya asi wona ereonowana i nonori wai Bada i wonei.
Ba Bada God i kaobeyei, “Gamosi ke nonori ba taupauma ke berisi.” Damanina ba Samuel Israel biyisi i wonisi, “Ereonowami ko veramaga ami ku meyaga.”
Sebare kesana bada kaikapona kana waba Kish, Benjamin rakarakana kamonai; Kish wai Abiel natuna ba Abiel wai Zero natuna ba Zero wai Becorath natuna ba Becorath wai Benjamin biyina, Aphia natuna.
Ba Kish natuna wai Saul komeruwana pusona kega kotoi Israel kamonai kona rutainina. I kaidagima wai pipiya i getawanisi.
Saul tamana Kish ana donkey mutusi si siwana wai, natuna Saul kurina i wona, “Saibisaibirina kesana ke urabai yabata kona nae ba donkey kona nuvenisi.”











Kona kaonai muri yai Saul ita botu, wai Bada Samuel i wonei,
“Niko marana kesanina maram, sebare kesana Benjamin biyina ani porai kurim. Ki boroi au pipiya Israel biyisi asi bada, ba au pipiya Philistia biyisi karisi yai ini yawasisi. Kairavina au pipiya asi tou bibaita kairavina a nonori ba a binuwanuwanisi.”











Damanina ba Samuel wairoro dubina i yauni ba Saul gayaminai i bosewai, i yaoni ba i wona, “Nikona a wosewosei basuna Bada i bineim ana pipiya Israel kuni badisi.
Karaku kuna kasibau taveyiku wai sebasebare ruwamo Rachel kana karawagai Zelza kupurinai Benjamin ana biparaparatai kuna pananisi. Sina wona kurim, ‘Donkey ko nuwenuwenisi wai si pananisi ba tamam kega e biyapoyena meyisi. Saba kom e biyapoyim ba e bitoirubim, “Mekabage natuku ana panani?” ’


Kona murinai kuna nae ku Gibeah God ana ku koya, namai Philistia biyisi asi basekwa e mamana wai, kuna riuriu wai peroperoveta kuna pananisi bopepeta gawarinai sina gaigakira ere asi gita, tambourine, durere sini biyakwarisi ba sina parapara ba sina rikuriku ba sini biperoveta wona.
Ba Kanuma Kaobaisiyena ere maragasina ina gakira kurim ba yabata koni peroveta wona ba, am yawasa ini waubirai.
Maranai nikosi wose sina tupuwa ba awaika God ini beyim wai ke wosei.
Ki nao ke nae ku Gilgal ba namai ana pananim wai suwara kapukapunina ba kam yabata suwarina tana puyo, saba kuni potapota yepo kao 7 ba ana botu wai ana wonim awaika kuna wosei.”
Saul i taibira Samuel iti sumarei, God Saul nuwanuwana i birai ba nikosi matakira ereonowasi kona kaonai si tupuwa,
Maranai Saul ana saibisaibirina yabata si verakasibau ku Gibeah, peroperoveta si verabeyisi ba God kanumina ere maragasina i riuni wai yabata si peroveta wona.
Maranai pipiya i iyabosi Saul si kuiri wai, si toiruba bibirana. “Awaika Kish natuna kurina i tupuwa, Saul yebo i peroveta kona?”
Sebare namai i mamana wai i kaobeya, “Ba tamasi kotoi?” Sisiyina i tupuwa, “Kata Saul kona peroperoveta yabata kona?”
Saul i peroveta wona i kakaba wai i gae ku bopepeta gawarina.
Saul abuna ana saibisaibirina yabata i toirubaisi, “Mekei ko nae?” Saul i wona, “Donkey ka nuwenuwenisi ba kega ka pananisi wai ka nae Samuel kurina.”
Saul abuna i wona, “Ke woniku, Samuel awaika i wonim?”
Saul i kaobeyei, “I wonikai kata matapa donkey si pananisi.” Saba ana bitaupauma kairavina Samuel i wonei wai kega abuna i mamatarei.
Samuel Israel biyisi i yorisi si notuwa ku Mizpa,
ba kurisi i wona, “Nikasike Bada Israel biyisi asi God i wona, ‘Israel biyisi Egypt biyisi kamosi yai a urabaisi a kasibau, ba dam mutusi si kasikasibigoyonimi wai yarosiai ai yawasimi.
Yauku ami God ami nuwapoya ba siniyara kamosi yai, ai taraparanimi, saba karaku koi sinikikiyiku, ba ami waina taupauma. Damanina ami rakaraka ba dam nunusi yai ko notuwa kuriku ba kom si kewakewai.’”
Maranai rakaraka ba dam ereonowasi si notuwa wai Benjamin ana dam i binei.
Damanina ba Benjamin ana dam si msi kasibau wai rakaraka nununai si kasibau ba Matri rakarakana kamonai sebasebare si kasibau wai Kish natuna Saul i binei. Ba si kinana wai kona kega nai.
Bada si toirubai, “Kona memei?” Ba Bada i wona, “Kona wai bobitaura ba sawara murisi yai i koba.”
Si vera si nuveni ba si panani wai si urabai si kasibau, pipiya naosi yai i msiri ba si kinani wai kona i kaidagima saki kega kotoi rutainina.
Samuel pipiya kurisi i wona, “Bada niko sebare i binei wai ko kinakinani kona? Sebarena nina kega kesana kotoi kamoti yai kona rutainina.” Pipiya ereonowasi si parara, “Taupauma ina ma saki!”
















Damanina Samuel pipiya kurisi i wona, “Ko botu tana nae ku Gilgal taupauma tani yoneyonena meyei.”
Damanina ereonowasi si nae ku Gilgal ba Saul Bada matanai si damaninei kata kona taupauma. Namai aba payapayaya si berena nuwanuba ba kam yabata suwarina Bada kurina, ba Saul ba Israel biyisi si nuwagaire.





































Samuel Saul i yegai, “Ku neganega Bada am God i kaotunetuneim wai gamona kega ku bosisirei; kuta bosisirei wai am basileiya Israel kamonai ita bobimaragata damanei.
Ba karaku am basileiya kega ina mana; saba karaku Bada pipiya nuwanuwanai ikesina i binei wai ana pipiya ini badisi, kairavina kom, Bada gamona kega ku bosisirei.”





























































Samuel Saul kurina i wona, “Yauku ikesiku mom Bada i poraiku ai boroim ana pipiya Israel asi taupauma, wai karaku niko wara, Bada karinai ke nonori.
Bada Maragata sakina nikasike i wona, ‘Amalek biyisi saroba ana berisi kairavina awaika Israel biyisi kurisi si wosei maranai Egypt yai si botubotu wai asi keta si gudui ba si ravisi.
Ko nae Amalek biyisi kona ravisi ba asi sawara ereonowasi kona reso. Kega kesana awaika ina mana, sebasebare, bibaine, pipiya gunaguna, pepeya, cow ba sheep, camel ba donkey ereonowasi koni kasi bunuwanisi.’”
Saul ana abiabiyisi i yorisi ku Telaim ba abiya kairavina i bobunagisi, 200,000 wai Israel tano abiabiyisi ba 10,000 Judah abiabiyisi.


Damanina ba Saul Amalek biyisi si kasibunuwanisi Havila ai ba i nae ku Shur, Egypt maramatanai.
Amalek biyisi asi taupauma si patumi, ba ana pipiya ereonowasi seri yai si kasibunuwanisi.
Saba Saul ba ana abiabiyisi Agag si nuwanuwani ba sheep, cow gaigairesi ba natunatusi bikampotasi ba sawara gaigairesi si yauna. Sawara goyogoyosi ereonowasi si kasibigoyonisi.
Damanina ba Bada Samuel kurina i sisiya,
“Ai nuwapoya kata awaika kairavina Saul a wosei i taupauma ba i msi kuputa ba awaika a wonei wai kega i wosei.” Samuel, i yagisi Bada kurina wai i tou maratom.
Ba Samuel i sukumara Saul ita nuveni saba si wonei kata Saul i nae ku Carmel. Namai kasa i kemai ikesina ana matakira ba i gakira ku Gilgal.
Maranai Samuel i verakasibau wai, Saul i wona, “Bada ini gairenim! Yauku God ana kaobiyoyobana a wosei.”
Saba Samuel i wona, “Ba awaika a nonori sheep ba cow te kwenekwene.”
Saul i kaobeyei, “Abiabiyisi Amalek biyisi karisi yai si yauna si botu, sheep ba cow gaigairesi si yauna puyobunuwa Bada am God kurina. Ba ereonowana wai ka kasibigoyoni.”
Samuel i wona Saul kurina, “Ke boterei! Awaika Bada God pomai i woniku wai ana wonim.” “Ke woniku.”
Samuel i wona, “Bagunai wata ku kitakitai kirena meyim saba kom wai Israel biyisi asi bada. Bada i boroim Israel kana taupauma.
Ba i poraim ba i kaotuneim, ‘Ke nae Amalek piragagoyo pipiyisi ke popora roboisi, ba yabata koni abiya ba sina momosa.’
Awaika kairavina Bada gamona kega ku bosisirei? Ba awaika kairavina sawara ku kita kirorowana ba ku sekwa yagina? Ba goyona Bada matanai ku wosei.”
Saul i wona, “Bada a bosisirei. A kasibau i woniku wai nanakasike a wosei, Amalek biyisi ai kasibunuwana roboisi ba asi taupauma Agag a yauni a botu.
Abiabiyisi sheep ba cow gaigairesi abiya kamonai si yauna si bosirei Gilgal ai sina puyobunuwa Bada am God kurina.”
Saba Samuel i kaobeyei, “Mekona Bada e wiwaini, bosisira kona suwara kapukapunina ba puyobunuwa? Bada ana waina bosisira kega puyobunuwa. Bitainabaenega wai i gaire kega bage puyobunuwa.
Bikawakasekase wai kesanina bage yapune. Netagegeyana nanakasike bage tarabibisaka bopepetina rutainina. Bada wonana kui sinikikiyei, wai yebo am bitaupauma i sinikikiyei.”



Damanina Samuel i taibira ita nae wai, Saul Samuel kana gara i botawani ba i taina sikai.
Ba Samuel kurina i wona, “Bada Israel ana basileiya karaku karimi yai i taina taveyei ba maturam i berei, kona pipiya gairena kega kom rutainim.
God kona Israel ana Kadara kega e bi kwarukwaruma kona ana nota ina birai; kona kega pipiya rutainisi, ba ana nota ina birai.”




Damanina ba Samuel i nae ku Rama, ba Saul i veramaga ana ku yove, Gibeah.
Samuel kega Saul i kinana meyei yepo i rabobo saba Saul kairavina i tou. Ba Bada God i yapoya saburere kata Saul i binei Israel biyisi asi taupauma.
Bada God Samuel kurina i wona, “Kega Saul kairavina kuna tou saki ba Israel asi taupauma Saul wai ai sinikikiyei. Olive wairoro ke yauni ba ke nae ku Bethlehem Jesse kurina. Natuna kesana a binei ini taupauma.”
Saba Samuel i wona, “Mekabage ana nae? Saul ina nonori wai ina kasibunuiku.” Bada i wona, “Cow kesana ke yauni ba ke wona, ‘A botu puyobunuwa ana wosei Bada kurina.’
Jesse ke wonei ina botu puyobunuwa kairavina ba ani beyim awaika kuna wosei. Pipiya ani beyim wai kairaviku ki boroi.”
Awaika Bada i wonei wai i wosei. Maranai i verakasibau ku Bethlehem wai, meyaga warawaraetesi si kinani wai si nagara. Si toiruba, “Nuwanubai ku botu kona?”
Samuel i kaobeya, “Eee, nuwanubai a botu ana puyobunuwa Bada kurina. Ko bobunaga meyim ba ko botu yabata tana puyobunuwa.” Damanina ba Jesse natunatuna yabata i bobunagisi ba i yorisi si nae si puyobunuwa.
Si verakasibau ba Samuel Jesse natuna iyarokona Eliab i kinani wai i nosi kata, “Damanina nikona Bada ana binebinena nina matanai e bimsiri.”
Saba Bada Samuel kurina i wona, “Kega ana kaidagima kona tupuwina kuna kinani, kairavina a bisinikikiyei. Pipiya awaika te kinakinani wai Bada kega kosi e kinakinana. Pipiya wai tupuwina e kinakinani, saba Bada wai nuwanuwana e kinakinani.”


Jesse natunatuna sebasebare asi 7 Samuel naonai si yewo si nae ba Samuel i wona, “Nikosi kega kesana Bada i binei.”
Damanina i toiruba, “Natunatum yebo mutusi te mamana kona kega?” Jesse i kaobeyei, “Murimurina dama e mamana, saba sheep e koyakoyagisi.” “Wasaga koi porai ina urabai ina botu. Kega tana makira yepo ina verakasibau.”
Kata i poraisi si urabai si botu. Kona wai, kinanina nuwarubarubana ba komeruwana pusona. Ba Bada i Samuel i wonei, “Sebarena damanina, ke bomsiri kuni boroi.”
Samuel wairoro i yauni ba warewaresina naosi yai i boroi, ba kona maranai Bada Kanumina maragasina i gakira David ku tepana. Kona murinai Samuel i nae ku Rama.
Karaku Bada God Kanumina Saul i kasibau taveyei, ba kanuma goyona Badai porai wai i bimagoyowei.







































































Mekabage wata Saul David i wonewonei ba i biporai ita wosei wai, ereonowana i wosewose kabitamni wai Saul i binei kata abiabiyisi asi bada kaikapona. Niko wose Saul i wosei wai pipiya ereonowasi ba Saul ana babada mutusi yabata si nuwagaire.

Bibaine si rikuriku maranai si tabora, “Saul abiya 1,000 i kasibunuisi, ba David 10,000 i kasibunuisi.”
Nikona Saul i wosei i yagisi saki, “Niko awaika? Te wonawona David 10,000 ba yauku 1,000 wata. Muri yai yebo sina wosei ini taupauma.”
Kona maranai David i nuwarauwei ba ana nota goyogoyosi wata kurina.
























































































David i nae ku Nob priest Ahimelek kurina. Ahimelek i kinani wai i nagara i kiroro i pokipokiyei ba i toiruba, “Awaika kairavina ikesim ku botu? Awaika kairavina kega kesana kotoi i ruwaim?”
David i kaobeyei, “Taupauma ana saibira a wosewosei. I woniku kega kesana kotoi ana wonei kata awaika kairavina yauku nina. Ba au pipiya wai, a wonisi memei sina pananiku.
Kam karimi yai kona kega, ba bread asi 5 kona kam mutusi gwabimi ai wai, kuta beriku?”
Ba priest Ahimelek i kaobeyei, “Bread mom kega, saba bread kaobaisiyena wata, kuna yauni abisiri yai am pipiya kega wasike kesana yabata si dauwa.”
David i kaobeyei, “Kega am nota ina kairagaraga. Maranai nikasike ka bowagawaga wai au pipiya kega bibaine kurisi te nenae. Ba yebo ka bowagawaga mom wai nanakasike. Kona kairavina kega nuwanuwam ina kairagaraga!”
Kam kega si mamana bread kaobaisiyena wata wai priest bread kaobaisiyena Tabernacle kamonai i mamana wai si berei ba kona kaonai wauna si tepari.







































































































































































































































Kona maranai Philistia biyisi Israel yabata sibi abiya ba Israel biyisi si vera ba pesarisi Gilboa koyanai si kasibunuwanisi.
Philistia biyisi Saul natunatuna koi si kwabinisi, ba natunatuna asi tonu Jonathan, Abinadab, ba Malkishua si kasibunuwanisi.
Saul gwabinai abiya i bita saki wai i sirage pidu ai si yowai.
Ana kapiya kabakabara i wonei, “Am seri yai ke gwari bunuiku. Kega au waina nikosi Philistia etenisi sina bogoyoiku ba sina kasibunuiku.” Saba ana kapiya kabakabara i nagara saki. Damanina Saul ana seri i yauni ba ku tepana i peku ba ikesina i gwari meyei ba i rabobo.
Ana kapiya kabakabara yebo ikesina i gwari bunu meyei, Saul i wosei wai kesanina ba i rabobo.






















































































































Damanina ba, Israel dam nununai, ereonowasi si notuwa David kurina ku Hebron ba si wona, “Yakai kona, kom, ama tupuwa ba ama tara.
Rorowa Saul i taupauma maranai, kom ama abiabiyisi ku binaovisi abiya kairavina, ba Bada kurim i wona kata, ‘Kom Israel biyisi kasi aba potapota ba asi bada.’”
Maranai Israel warawaraetesi, si botu David kurina ku Hebron ba, debai bidamanina maragasina Bada matanai si wosei ba, David si boroi Israel kana taupauma.
David kana bodu 30 ba bitaupauma i dagui ba bodu 40 rubana i bada.












































Maranai David ana bitaupauma yovenai i mabinubai murinai, kana abiya si tompipini wai Bada i bopapari ba i yakam kabitam.
Ba peroveta Nathan kurina i wona, “Yauku nina yove gairena cedar keyaminai si bowai wai a mamana, saba God ana Bidamanina Maragasina Dedewagina tent kamonai e mamana.”
Nathan i kaobeyei, “Awaika wata am notai e mamana wai ke wosei kairavina Bada wai kom karimi yai.”
Kona pomnai Bada Nathan kurina, i wona,
“Ke nae ba au saibisaibirina David ke wonei, ‘Bada nikasike, i wona, “Kata kom naki au aba mamana yovena kuna bowai?” ’


Au saibisaibirina David ke wonei, ‘Bada Maragata Sakina nikasike e wonawona, “Kom kwapu kamonai sheep kasi aba potapota ba, a uraba kasibauwim au pipiya Israel biyisi asi bada.
Memei wata ku yewo wai yauku yabata, ba kam abiya naomi yai a kasiyaraga taveyisi. Ba karaku kam waba ana bokabari nanakasike bage pipiya kaikaposi niko dobu ai rutainisi.
Ba au pipiya Israel biyisi asi gawara ana berisi ba ana tere damanisi kata sina kwanatu ba kega kotoi ini bubuwisi. Pipiya goyogoyosi kega sina bobisipuwena meyisi, rorowa si wosewosei wai nanakasike,
ba si wosewosei yepo i botu babada a bineisi kata au pipiya Israel biyisi sita potaisi. Ba yebo kami abiya ereonowasi karisi yai biyakam ana berimi. Ba yauku mom am yove ana bowa damanei. Maranai kuna rabobo ba tamatamam yabata koni biyakam murinai, kamomi yai natum kesana ana binei wasam ini taupauma ba ana basileiya ana tere damanei.
Maranai kuna rabobo ba tamatamam yabata koni biyakam murinai, kamomi yai natum kesana ana binei wasam ini taupauma ba ana basileiya ana tere damanei.
Kona mom God ana yove ina bowai kau Waba kairavina, ba ana basileiya aba makimakirina ana terei damanei.
Yauku wai tamana ba kona wai natuku. Maranai goyona ina wosei wai, saroba ana berei ba ana kaobitotori nanakasike bage tama natuna kurina e wosewosei.
Saba au nuwayauyauna kega meyana karinai ana yauna taveyei, nanakasike matami yai Saul karinai a yauna taveyei.
Ba am yove ba am basileiya mataku ai sina madamana ba, am aba makimakira ana tere damanei.” ’”
Nathan awaika ereonowana aba kinakinanai, God i beyei wai David i waraberei.






























































Kaburutiti maranai, bodu patepatena kamonai, tautaupauma si kasikasibau abiya kairavina, David ana abiya badana Joab, ba taupauma ana pipiya ba Israel abiabiyisi ereonowasi i poraisi. Kata Ammon biyisi si poporisi ba Rabbah si garapipini, saba David wai Jerusalem yai i madamana.
Rabisi kesana nubanai, David ana aba dudauwa gawarinai i bomsiri ba, taupauma yovena wadakupunai i yewoyewo neubuwa, ba i kinana i gakira wai wasike i bitowatowa wai i kinani. Wasikena wai kepamara pusona.
Ba pipiya kesana i porai iti toiruba kata kona kotoi. Pipiyina i wona, “Kona wai Eliam natuna, Bathsheba ba Hitti sebare Uriah kaowana.”
Damanina ba David kawariyonayona i porai sita urabai. Ba wasikena i botu kurina wai yabata si dauwa ba i nae ana ku yove.
Bathsheba i bopanani kata i manawa wai, David ana wara i porai, i wona, “Yauku a manawa.”
Damanina, David wara nikasike i porai Joab kurina, “Hitti biyina, Uriah ki porai kuriku.” Kata Joab i porai David kurina.
Maranai Uriah i verakasibau wai, David i toirubai, kata Joab ba abiabiyisi damanina kona, ba abiya si riuni wai mekabage e veravera. Ba Uriah i kaobeyei i wona, “Damanina wata.”
Damanina ba David i wona, “Ke gakira am ku yove ba kuni yakam mara yogina.” Kata Uriah, taupauma yovena i kasibau taveyei ba kana puyo murinai David i porai.
Saba Uriah kega i nae ana ku yove ba, taupauma yovena matam ketanai, aba potapotasi yabata si dauwa.
Maranai David i nonori kata Uriah kega i nae ana ku yove wai, i toirubai, “Awaika i goyo? Niko mara veoromina rabarabai ku mamana ba, awaika kairavina kega ku nae am ku yove?”
Ba Uriah i kaobeya, “Israel ba Judah abiabiyisi ba Bidamanina Maragasina Dedewagina wai tent kamonai te mamana ba au bada Joab ana pipiya yabata matarai si rubasekwa te mamana. Mekabage yauku ata nae au ku yove ba ata kam ba ata toma ba, kaowaku yabata kata dauwa? A bisuwonim nikona kega rubana ana wosei!”
Damanina David kurina, i wona, “Karaku nina ke mana ba maram ani poraim kuna veramaga.” Kata Uriah Jerusalem yai i mana kao ruwamo.
David ana waina wai i bababai yabata si kamdauwa ba i toma neganegai. Ba yebo kona pomnai kega i nae ana ku yove ba ana bada, ana saibisaibirisi yabata si dauwa mena.
Mara i tom wai, David wara pepai i kirumi Joab kurina ba, Uriah i porai i kabari i nae.
Warana kamonai i kiruma i wona, “Abiya memena i rakata saki ba e boborabora wai Uriah naonai ke terei ba koi sumarei sina kasibunui.”
Joab i kuiri memena abiabiyisi maragata sakiyisi, meyaga kaikapona parinai si biabiya wai Uriah namai i terei.
Maranai meyaga kaikapona kana pipiya si kasibau ba Joab ana pipiya yabata si rauwa wai David ana abiabiyisi mutusi si rabobo. Hitti biyina Uriah, yebo i rabobo.








Maranai Bathsheba wara i nonori kata kaowana Uriah i rabobo wai, kairavina i nuwapoya ba i tou.
Ba kaowana kairavina i nuwapoya ba i tou i kakaba murinai, David wara i porai wai i botu ana ku yove ba i yauni i kaowanei ba, natuna sebare i tuwei. Saba niko wose i wosei wai Bada kega i nuwagaire.
Bada peroveta Nathan i porai, David kurina, ba maranai i botu kurina wai, i wona, “Sebasebare asi ruwamo meyaga kesana kamonai si mamana. Sebarena kesana marimariyina ba kesana moyamoyakina.
Sebare marimariyina ana aba payapayaya si pesara saki,
ba sebare moyamoyakina karinai wai kega awaika ba, lamb wasikena wotuna kesanaikei i gimoni. Ba i potai kata natunatuna koi karinai si rakata, ba yabata si kamkam ba si tomatoma, ba yebo tokaranai i dudauwa. Nanakasike bage natuna wasikena.
Kao kesana wagawaga biyina i botu marimariyina ana ku yove. Saba sebare marimariyina kega ana waina kata ana aba payapayaya kesana ita kasibunui kam kana wagawaga kairavina ita bobunagi. Saba sebare moyamoyakina ana lamb wasikena i yauni ba kam i bobunagi kana wagawaga kairavina.”
David i yagisi saki, sebare marimariyina kurina ba i wona, “Bada yawayawasina kana wabai, niko sebare ina rabobo!
Niko wose goyo tavetaveyina i wosei ba, kega i kamyosukuwei, kairavina lamb asi 4 ini tepari sebare moyamoyakina kurina.”
Damanina Nathan, David i wonei, “Sebarena wai kom! Bada Israel asi God, nikasike e wonawona, ‘Kom ai boroim kata Israel asi taupauma ba, Saul nimana kamonai a bopaparim.
Am bada ana yove a berim ba kaokaowana ku nimam a terisi. Israel ba Judah asi basileiyisi a berim. Abisiri yai nikona i yogiyogi saki wai, yebo kaikapo sakina ata berim.
Awaika kairavina, Bada wonana kui kasikotobi ba matanai niko wose goyona ku wosei? Ba Hitti biyina Uriah, Ammon biyisi asi seri yai ku kasibunui ba, kaowana ku yauni i karimi yai.
Kona kairavina, karaku ba nakai i nae wai, niko seri kega am yove ina kasibau taveyei, kairavina kui gigimiku ba, Uriah kaowana ku yauni, i karimi yai.’
Bada nikasike e wonawona, ‘Am yove damana kamonai kam biuwa ina botu kurim. Ba matami yai kaokaowam, kao boraborai ana yauna ba sebare kesana gwabimi yai ana berei ba debai yabata sina dauwa.
Kom baibuni ai nikona ku wosei, saba kom kurim wai debai, Israel biyisi matasi yai ana wosei ina tupuwa.’”
Damanina David Nathan kurina i wona, “Yauku Bada kurina piragagoyo a wosei.” Nathan i kaobeyei, “Bada am piragagoyona i yauna taveyei. Ba kega kuna rabobo.
Saba niko wose ku wosei wai Bada kana waba ku gigimi, kona kairavina, wai natum sebare kuni tuwei wai ina rabobo.”
Nathan i veramaga ana ku yove murinai, Uriah kaowana David karinai pipiyaikei i tuwei wai, Bada gubaga raoboraobo i porai kurina kata i gubaga saburere.
David, God i baba kuwakuwayei pipiyaikei ana yawasa kairavina. I siya ba i riu ana ku yove kamona ba pomai wai tano ai i dudauwa maratom.
Warawaraetesi ana yove yai, parinai si msiri ba si babai ita bomsiri yabata sita kam saba i totoyana ba kega ana waina yabata sita kam.
Kao kana bi 7 kamonai pipiyaikei i rabobo. Ba David ana saibisaibirisi wonina si nagarei. Si wona, “Pipiyaikei yawayawasinai wai, David kurina tabi sisiya ba kega i nonorita. Mekabage tana wonei kata pipiyaikei i rabobo? Muri yai ba ina kayo bisiragena meyei.”
David ana saibisaibirisi i kinanisi kosi wata si biponasimsim wai, damina i yauni kata pipiyaikei i rabobo, wai i toiruba, “Kata pipiyaikei i rabobo kona?” Ba si kaobeyei, “Eee, pipiyaikei i rabobo.”
Damanina David tano ai i dudauwa wai i bomsiri ba i towa bunabunaga, i mutu, ba i gara rutaveyei, ba i nae Bada ana ku yove ba i bopepetei. Kona murnai i veramaga ana ku yove ba i baba wai kam si bobunagi ba i kam.
Ana saibisaibirisi si toirubai, “Awaika kairavina nikasike ke wosewose? Pipiyaikei yawayawasinai wai ku bisiya ba ku tutou, saba karaku pipiyaikei i rabobo wai ku bomsiri ba ke kamkam!”
David i kaobeya, “Pipiyaikei yawayawasina i mamana wai, ai siya ba a tou. A nosi bage Bada iti nuwanuwaniku ba pipiyaikei yawasina ita mana.
Saba karaku kona wai i rabobo, awaika kairavina ani siya? Rubana ana yawasa ani neveramagei kona? Kurina ana nae saba kona kega rubana ina veramaga kuriku.”
Damanina ba David kaowana Bathsheba i morumorubi, ba i nae yabata si dauwa. Ba i tuwa wai natuna sebare ba kana waba si yorei Solomon. Ba Bada pipiyinaikei i nuwayauyauni,
ba Bada i nuwayauyauni kairavina wona i porai peroveta Nathan kurina kata sebareikei kana waba ita yorei Jedidiah.


































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































Nikona wai God Natuna, Iesu Keriso warana gairena dagudaguna.
Peroveta Isaiah i kirumi wai nanakasike, “God i wona, ‘Au kawariyonayona ani porai ini nao, am keta ina bobunagi.’
Sebare kesana kupura momnai e paraparara, ‘Bada kairavina, keta ko bobunaga! Ba totorinai ina yewo.’”
Kata John kupura momna i babataito, ba pipiya i wonewonisi, “Ami piragagoyosi ai koi nuwabirabira, ba kona babataito wai God ami piragagoyosi ina notataveyisi.”
Judea biyisi ereonowasi ba Jerusalem meyagina pipiyisi ereonowasi si kasibau si nae John kurina, ba Jordan okowinai asi piragagoyo si tombaubaunisi ba si babataito.
Ba John kana gara wai camel sini korokoronai si wosei, wai i kotei, ba abapayapayaya kwapirina i kikiruwei, ba kana kam sidim ba dudau i kamkam.
Pipiya kurisi i raumamara i wona, “Sebare kesana muriku ai ina botu kona wai i maragata saki kega bage yauku, kega gaireku ba ata borunoma kana kae sumasuma ata tombaunisi.
Yauku okowai a babataitoimi, saba kona wai Kanuma Kaobaisiyenai ina babataitoimi.”
Kona maranai, Iesu Nazareth meyagina, Galilee kupurinai i botu, ba John Jordan okowinai Iesu i babataitoi.
Ba Iesu okowai i rupaira i gegae ku tepa, ba sapama i kitai i tamotatara ba Kanuma Kaobaisiyena kinanina bage bunebune i gaigakira kurina.
Ba gamo sapamai i wona, “Kom Yauku natuku au nuwayauyauna kom ai ba a binuwagaire.”
Ba yagiyagina wata, Kanuma Kaobaisiyena i naovei i kasibau ku kupura momna.
Ba namai garagara aba payapayaya yabata si mana kao 40, ba Satan i botu i sakariyei. Ba God ana aneya si botu si baisi.
John si tere riuwei ku patuma yovena murinai, Iesu i veramaga ku Galilee ba God warana gairena e botubotu wai i rumamarei.
Ba i wona, “Mara i botu, ba God ana basileiya i neratui! Koi nuwabirabira ba wara gairena koni geruwei!”
Kao kesana Iesu Galilee torenai i yewo i nenae, ba Simon waresina Andrew yabata i kinanisi sewari si bigarui kairavina kosi wai banobanotisi.
Iesu i wonisi, “Ko botu kona kibiku ba yauku ani beyebeyeimi mekabage pipiya kona konaisi.”
Ba yagiyagina wata asi sewari si sumarei ba si kibi.
I yewo i nae yoginaikei ba Zebedee natunatuna James ba John i kinanisi, wakai asi sewari si yanuyanumi.
Iesu i yorisi wai yagiyagina tamasi Zebedee ana saibisaibirisi yabata si sumarisi ba kona si kibi.
Ba si nae ku Capernaum, ba Sabath marana i botu wai Iesu ku dugu yovena i riu ba bibeyebeyena i dagui.
Ba pipiya iyabosi ana bibeyebeyena si nonori wai si wareyei, kairavina ana bibeyebeyena ere maragasina kega bage kairuwana bibeyebeyena biyisi rutanisi.
Kona maranai, sebare kanuma goyona i bonuwei wai i riu ku Jew biyisi asi ku dugu yovena ba i para,
“Iesu Nazareth biyim, a kuirim kom kotoi, kom God ana kawariyonayona kaobaisiyem, awaika ke wiwaini kuna wosei kurikai, ku botu kuna kasibigoyonikai kona?”
Saba Iesu kanuma goyona i kaotunei i wona, “Kawam e pota, ba nao sebare ke kasibau taveyei!”
Kata kanuma goyona ere yagisina sebare i gusui, ba ere paraparana i kasibau taveyei.
Ba pipiya tupasi si wareyei, ba si dagui si bikaoboneyana, “Niko awaika, bibeyebeyena wauna kona? Niko sebare maragata karinai wai kanuma goyogoyosi e kaotuneisi wai te bosisirei.”
Ba Iesu warana yagiyagina wata Galilee kupurina ereonowana i bonuwei.
Maranai Jew biyisi asi dugu yovena si kasibau taveyei wai, yagiyagina wata James ba John yabata si nae Andrew ba Simon asi ku yove.
Ba Iesu i verakasibau wai si wonei, kata Simon rawana wasikena i gubaga saki ana gawarai i dudauwa.
I nae kurina, yarona i yauni, ba i taina bimsiri wai i yawasa, ba i dagui i bosaibirisi.
Kona rabisinai kao i gakira murinai, pipiya gubagubagisi ba iyabosi kanuma goyogoyosi kamosi yai ereonowasi si yaunisi si botu Iesu kurina.
Ba pipiya pesarisi nao meyaga kaikaponai yove naonai si gaenisi.
Ba Iesu kasi gubaga bubausi yai i yawasisi, ba kanuma goyogoyosi pesarisi i kasibaunisi. Ba kanumisi kega i damainisi kata awaika siti sisiyei kairavina si kuiri kona wai kotoi.
Maratom didibarinai muri yai mara ita ru yasegana, Iesu i sikwana ba yove i kasibau taveyei. Ba i nae kupura momnai ba namai i rupari.
Saba Simon turaturana yabata si kasibau kona si nuwenuweni.
Ba si panani wai si wonei, “Pipiya ereonowasi kom te nuwenuwenim.”
Saba Iesu i kaobeyisi i wona, “Tana nae ku meyaga mutusi, kosi yebo kamosi yai ana rumamara. Kona kairavina a botu.”
Kata Galilee kupurina i yewo roboisi, Jew biyisi asi dugu yovesi kamosi yai i rumamara ba kanuma goyogoyosi i bikasibaunisi.
Sebare kesana leprosy sininai ba i botu Iesu kurina, i maere sogasoga ba i baba tupetupeni kata iti baisi, i wona, “Am waina wai kuni yawasiku.”
Iesu nuwanuwana i poya sakiyei, ba i bororona i borubai ba i wonei, “Au waina, ke yawasa!”
Yagiyagina wata leprosy i kasibau taveyei, ba sebarena i yawasa.
Damanina ba Iesu sisiya padapadana i berei ba i pora taveyei.
Ba Iesu i wona, “Kega kesana kotoi ketai kuna wonei, saba totorina ke nae priest kurina ba ikesina sinim ina kinani, ba ereonowasi sini geruwei kata kom ku yawasa wai, ke nae Moses puyo i wonei wai nanakasike ke puyobunuwa.”
Saba sebarena i nae ba kupura tupana i sisiya neubuwei wai koroto si kuira roboi kairavina kega rubana Iesu debai ita kasibau ku meyaga ba i ma taveyana, saba pipiya memei wata si mamana wai ereonowasi si botubotu kurina.
Maranai Iesu i veramaga ku Capernaum, ba warana i rakata kata kona wai yove yai.
Kata pipiya ereonowasi si botu si kesanisi wai kega memei gawara masarena i mamana, matarai kona matamketai, ba Iesu i rumamara kurisi.
Kona maranai sebasebare asi bata, sebare digadigana si kabari si botu Iesu kurina.
Saba koroto i rakata saki wai kega rubarubana sebarena sita yauni sita riu kurina, wai si gae ku wadakupuna ba si rebui ba sebarena ana aba dudauwai Iesu naonai si tere kirei.
Maranai Iesu asi bigeruwana i kinani wai sebarena i wonei, “Natuku am piragagoyosi a notataveyisi.”
Saba bibeyebeyena biyisi mutusi nai si mamana wai ikesisi kamosi yai si nuwanuwasuya.
“Kata awaika kairavina niko sebare nikasike e bisisiya? God ikesina wata piragagoyo ina notataveyana!”
Iesu yagiyagina wata nuwa sinenai i kuiri kata kosi wai awaika si nuwanuwasuyei, wai i wonisi, “Awaika kairavina nikasike ko nuwanuwasuya?
Mekona tapeyanina digadigana tana wonei, ‘Am piragagoyo a notataveyesi’ kona, ‘Ke bomsiri, ba am yagoro ke yauni ba ke yewo’?
